The remainder of the board contains blank squares for you to complete.\r\n\r\nYou will need to use all your powers of deductive reasoning to solve the unlimited supply of boards that Sudoku can generate. Sudoku supports the ability to mark each board square with possible moves to aid in the puzzle solving. Sudoku also supports the ‘cross hatch’ marking aid to solving puzzles.\r\n\r\nAll boards generated are symmetrical and have a single solution making them pure game boards. Sudoku also supports the popular game variation whereby the diagonals may only contain one instance of each piece.\r\n\r\nSudoku includes a lightning fast puzzle solver able to solve any external  puzzle.
